               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 北美華人家庭特殊教育兒童分享交流區
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 為確保本社團品質與社員隱私，所有申請加入者（含被邀請者）必須為特教兒家長本人，或特殊教育領域專家。 若您懷疑自己小孩有問題 學齡前&gt; 請找小兒科醫生, 轉介專家討論 學齡期間&gt; 請找學區輔導中心安排鑑定 請務必了解: 本社團為特教家長互助園地, 為尊重團員隱私, 不希望非家長, 及非專家參加. 申請者務請私訊回答下列問題，未答者將刪除其申請。 專家：請敘述專業以及接觸特殊兒童的經驗. 及執業州 (如 心理治療師 德州) 家長：請簡單介紹小孩情況 (如:小孩 性別 年紀 診斷 居住州) (如 女兒 十歲 自閉症 加州) ****************************************** 本社團宗旨為提供有特殊孩童家庭支持和分享平台，歡迎有任何學習,行為,發展相關障礙孩童的家庭及提供這些孩童服務的專業人員加入! 無論是想要尋找資料, 分享教養酸甜苦辣, 詢問其他社員成功經驗, 都很歡迎發文. 發文時請大家務必遵守以下的基本版規: 1. 在發文留言的時候, 請遵守基本禮貌. 請勿任意批評, 取笑, 挑釁, 吵架, 人身攻擊. 2. 社團不能徵人, 打商業還有私人買賣廣告. 3. 如果想要分享文章, 請先詢問發文者的同意在分享. 4. 每個小孩的早療師們用的方法都不一樣, 請大家在討論的時候, 不要有強烈個人成見. 5. 這是個不公開的社團, 也是讓各位爸媽可以放心地在社內討論. 因此, 隱私非常非常的重要. 請勿擅自截圖. 請大家互相尊重彼此的隱私權. 6. 請勿線上問診. 在社團裡面, 大家可以提供意見想法, 可是如果有什麼顧慮, 有請專業相關人員正式評估諮商比較妥當. 7. 管理員有權刪除任何不妥的發文. 8. 如果有任何問題或建議, 歡迎私訊管理員: LR Annette Bei Shan Chien CJ Chiang
                </div>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Free Homeschool Ideas
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 We are living in uncharted times. People are, in some cases, being tossed into homeschooling without any direction. Some are choosing to homeschool with the intent of going back to public school when it feels comfortable to them. As an educator turned homeschooling mom, I feel I have an amazing opportunity to share what I know and have learned. As a group, we can share our resources, ideas, and yes support. At the end of the day, our job as parents is to raise our children the best we can. We who know the homeschooling world should love our neighbor and support each other. What if there is one mom who isn't sure of herself until another mom, a veteran, comes along and just gives her a little positivity? Is that so hard? It seems we are latching on to the negative when we should be embracing the positive opportunities. I created this group as a place to pin my homeschool stuff. What started as a personal bulletin board has grown into an unbelievable group of moms, dads, grandparents, relatives, and even friends who, at the end of the day want exactly what I want, which is to help others and be the best they can be. I am proud of this little Facebook group and I will continue to work at it with all my heart. I hope you find something helpful and as always, please conduct yourself in an appropriate manner. Rude, offensive, and off-topic posts will be deleted.
                </div>

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 本團成立宗旨在分享申請美國大學時的一些資訊和相關講座等等，每個孩子不同，所考量的範圍也不一樣，申請大學也沒有公式可以套用，希望有經驗的家長們也能不吝分享有用的資訊，謝絕人頭帳號，廣告戶（謝絕PFA 成員）加入，一經發現即刻請出團，恕不另通知。 發言時希望大家能注意下列事項： 1請保持友善和禮貌 打造友善的環境是所有人的責任。請尊重他人。適度的辯論是合乎常情的，但別忘了保持友善。 2禁止促銷或發佈垃圾訊息 施比受更有福，請多多為社團貢獻實用內容。我們不允許自我推銷、垃圾訊息、不相關的連結。 3禁止仇恨言論或霸凌 確保所有人都能感到安心。我們不允許任何形式的霸凌行為，也無法容忍有關種族、宗教、文化、性取向、性別或個性的嘲笑留言。 4尊重所有人的隱私 加入社團就必須培養成員間的信任感。雖然開誠布公的討論有助於社團成長、茁壯，但也要注意到敏感議題和個人隱私，請勿四處張揚社團討論的內容。 謝謝大家的合作！
                </div>
               </div>

                 【菜鳥新移民】美國F, H1B, EB簽證討論區
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 本社團成立的目的, 在於協助並且提供一個平台, 給想要將來在美國長期發展的台灣的留學生們, 提供一個能互相交換訊息的討論區, 請版友們務必將發言鎖定在學生簽證, 工作簽證H1B, 以及職業移民EB-1到EB-5的範圍內, 謝謝大家配合. 版規 01. 發言時請尊重他人，僅就事實陳述，勿攻擊或汙衊任何對象。 02. 本社團只能針對美國學生F簽證, 工作簽證H, E1, E2, 以及職業移民類別EB-1, EB-2, EB-3, EB-4, EB-5提出相關問題詢問討論, 違反者將刪文, 情節嚴重者會被請出社團. 03. 本社團保留刪除留言與取消團員資格之權力，以維護社團正常運作與保障團員權益。 04.請大家儘量針對相關主題在各區內發言。 05.請就簽證移民相關問題進行發問討論，禁止任何廣告或是投資移民項目宣傳。

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 台灣博士在美國 … 學校待太久
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 有鑑於台灣人在美國的博士，還有學術界正處於一個青黃不接的階段。 眼看著上一輩的台灣教授都慢慢走向退休的年齡，中間有很大的斷層。年輕一輩的人面臨大陸或是印度人的強勢競爭。因為當我看到別的學校的DEAN大量拉拔自己國家的人的時候，台灣人的勢力慢慢削弱，我覺得我應該做點甚麼事情。 本社團一個提供台灣人在美國的博士、博士後、博班學生、ABD、教授、或是對念博士有興趣的交流園地。 請詳閱一下入團規定，若無法同意，或是沒有回答入團問題，版主保留刪除團員之權利: • 本社團只開放台灣人加入，敬請見諒 • 本特團只開放博士、博士生、有興趣攻讀博士的團員加入，申請者必須說明入團理由。 • 申請期間請取消隱私設定，版主審核過後，即可設回。 臉書無個人資料提供審核，一律無法加入。 • 為了維護社團正常運作，管理員保留刪除留言和取消團員資格的權利。 •請勿互相攻擊，請互相尊重彼此的想法 目的: 本社團最主要目的是提供學術交流、拉拔台灣人，讓台籍博士的勢力可以在美國日漸壯大。 討論涵蓋範圍如下，只要是跟博士相關議題皆可: 1. 如何申請美國博士班、如何在博士班生存 2. 博士畢業後出路和選擇、如何找工作 3. 如何申請終身教職工作、學校的型態有哪些、薪資如何 4. 博士畢業後在業界工作 5. 博士班心路歷程 6. 如何申請Grant，Grant合作 7. 如何發表Journal Paper、Journal Paper 跨領域合作 8. 學術圈生態、升等 【自我介紹】: https://www.facebook.com/groups/1643990659203936/permalink/1644143615855307/ 
                </div>
               </div>

                 Montessori Materials - Buy &amp; Sell - Product Reviews - Printables &amp; DIY
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 A place to ask about and advise on the value, quality and cost of Montessori teaching materials, suppliers and manufacturers. If you know of any special offers or discounts, please post them too. Or if you've written a blog post with an extensive review of materials, feel free to post a link. Also, please ask the group if you can't decide which materials to buy, make yourself or leave out altogether. Let’s help each other make wise purchases! If you have Montessori materials to sell or are looking for used items, then you may post in this group to locate a buyer or seller.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 大紐約地區臺灣校友會 Association of Taiwanese Alumni in Greater New York (ATANY）係非營利、非政治、非宗教性組織。其成立之目的在團結大紐約地區之留美臺灣校友，提供管道輔助各校友以俾服務臺灣留美校友，同時本會將舉辦各種服務性、學術性、聯誼性活動，以達增進各校學友之情誼為宗旨。 Association of Taiwanese Alumni in Greater New York (ATANY) was founded by former board members of Federation of Taiwanese Students Associations in Greater New York (FTSANY) in 2003. It is a non-profit, non-political, &amp; non religious organization. The primary goal of ATANY is to build a more unified community for Taiwanese alumni through social, cultural, and academic activities. Although most ATANY members are young professionals and graduate students, individuals of all ages, races, and nationalities are welcome. Photo Credit: http://vchin.viewbook.com/

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Kindergarten &amp; First Grade Teaching Ideas
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to our community! Kindergarten &amp; First Grade Teaching Ideas is a safe community where you can ask questions, offer support, and get actionable ideas for improving your teaching. Of course, we have a few rules to keep this space as focused and helpful as possible. Make sure you check them out to learn just how to get the most from our community! New? Let me introduce myself! I’m Anna Geiger, a former teacher (M.Ed.) now raising my six kids and supporting educators through my website, The Measured Mom. My site offers thousands of free resources for teaching preschool through third grade. You can check it out here: https://www.themeasuredmom.com/ Like what you see? Consider joining my membership site, where I release new printables, quick video trainings, and no-print resources every month. Learn more about The Measured Mom Plus here: https://membership.themeasuredmom.com/ This space is the place for you to get support, ask questions, and ultimately be the best teacher you can be while still having time to enjoy the rest of your life. HERE'S HOW THIS GROUP WORKS: Please DO NOT post self-promotions or spam. Links to your own website, business, and other Facebook groups are not allowed. Please DO be kind and courteous. We have a zero-tolerance policy for name calling, shaming, or bullying. Please DO NOT post links to files. If you'd like to share a link to a free online resource, post the link (not file) so others can download it for themselves. Do note that group admins may post files courtesy of The Measured Mom. Please DO NOT send private messages to admins or members of this group. Please DO NOT post or seek requests for Donors Choose, Go Fund Me, etc. Please STICK TO TEACHING. We look forward to getting to know you, but we ask that most posts pertain to teaching kindergarten and first grade. Posts entirely off-topic (and anything about politics!) may be swiftly deleted. Please DO post about your teaching joys and challenges so your fellow educators can support you. Please DO connect and collaborate, share your ideas, and engage with other awesome educators. We are a place of support and celebration! 
                </div>
               </div>

                 Montessori at Home (0 to 3 years)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The world's largest Montessori online platform connecting families from all over the world! A community of like-minded Montessori parents with a child aged from birth to 3. This community will support you on your journey in parenting and raising tomorrow's children. Create a Montessori home environment for children aged from birth to 3 and learn how to guide children to build life-skills. It is a place to share Montessori ideas, questions, materials and general Montessori experiences. Together we can raise a future generation of children who are mindful, confident, independent and able to self-regulate, laying a foundation for life. Please ensure that posts and comments are ON TOPIC and are RESPECTFUL. We have a number of qualified Montessori directresses within the group, as well as parents experienced in the method as applied in the home, but everyone is welcome to share and learn from each other.                  加州州立大學長堤分校台灣同學會(CSULB-TSA)提供大家一個機會和其他國家的朋友們分享彼此的歷史、文化、知識及經歷。同時，台灣同學會也會努力推廣台灣文化，讓更多來自不同國家的朋友們更認識台灣。 台灣同學會的夥伴們秉持服務的熱忱，盡心地幫助來到CSULB唸書的同學們，使同學們能夠很快的熟悉校園及周遭的環境。台灣同學會是一個團結且溫馨的大家庭，十分歡迎所有的同學們加入我們。 各位朋友們，如果你有任何問題需要我們的幫助，所有台灣同學會的幹部們會非常樂意的協助你，同時也希望你在CSULB有一個非常好的開始，並且好好地享受美好的校園生活。 Website:https://sites.google.com/site/csulbtsasite P.S. 我們這個網站是提供各位同學一個資源來發問, 互相幫忙, 以及交流的. 如果要打廣告, 請先經過我們的幹部同意才可張貼. 如有任何疑問, 歡迎與我們聯絡. 此外, 網站設定已更改, 如果有任何不便的地方, 請多多包涵. 謝謝.               <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Special Education Teachers
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome! Read to the end please for your own benefit. 1. This group is only for teachers and paraprofessionals working in the schools, Aides, OT, PT, SLP, etc. If you're not a teacher, close to becoming one or a paraprofessional please delete yourself before an admin has to. Nothing personal but this group was intended for teachers as a safe discussion area. 2. Report anyone who is not supposed to be in the group or who is not being respectful or someone who is spamming the group. *The report feature works very well. Admins can decide to keep, delete, or delete &amp; block! *Admins can delete any post but posters can also delete their post at any time (this doesn’t mean all evidence is gone, screen shots and photos can exist) 3. Maintain confidentiality of your students. 4. Be courteous and encouraging to your colleagues in the group. 5. Use appropriate and professional language but also don't be offended if someone uses a term or phrasing you dislike (unless it is clearly inappropriate, please report that). 6. Stay on topic, special education. 7. No spam in the group &amp; if selling beneficial special education related products (like from your tpt) on the feed DO NOT post it more than once in 48 hours! PLEASE post any FREE items you find that are awesome! No posts selling items not related to education or support of those with disabilities. Thanks again. ***Disclaimer. This is a closed group, not private. It will show that you are a member on your page. Colleagues/Admin from your school/area may also be members so please be mindful of what you post. Social Media can be wonderful but it can also be harmful to your career if you are caught saying negative things, being unprofessional, or getting close to confidentiality lines. Delete isn’t foolproof (once it’s out there, you can’t go back, people can take screen shots and pictures). **If anyone has any questions, please tag or PM admins: Laura Elaine Bertolucci Kim Smart or Valerie Cochran OR Moderator: Robin Rogers Thank you!
                </div>

                </div>

                 ***** PLEASE READ! ***** WELCOME! This is a group where homeschool MOMS using Fun Schooling With Thinking Tree Books (Dyslexia Games) by Sarah Janisse Brown can meet for fellowship, guidance, and ideas. Conversation should be related to TTT/Dyslexia Games and homeschooling please, though prayer requests are welcome. Please refrain from political related posts / discussion. There are many, many political based groups in which you can join and participate in. Group Owner / Admin: Melle Fischer Creator / Admin: Sarah Janisse Brown Admin / Ambassador : Linda Beltran Admin / Ambassador : Krystal Branom Moderator / Ambassador: Jennilyn Roll Chaplin Admin / Ambassador / Book Show Organizer &amp; Official UBAM Consultant for The Thinking Tree: Amanda Goldman Sarah’s current UBAM link is —&gt;&gt; https://l7975.myubam.com/1469316 (Should say: Sarah Janisse Brown’s Fun-Schooling w/ Usborne Books &amp; More at check out). Guidelines: - This group is for MOMS only. No men, no teens. - This group is NOT for the purpose of self-promotion or advertising (blogs, websites, groups, pinterest, etc). NO link dropping or Affiliate link posts. This includes posts, videos, links etc. All such posts will be deleted without warning. Our Admin, Amanda Goldman is the official Usborne Books &amp; More (UBAM) Consultant for The Thinking Tree and will share Sarah’s Approved Links when relevant. - If you have a specific blog / video post that specifically relates to TTT/Dyslexia Games, we do welcome a direct link to that post. If a member asks for help/advice, and you know a link that will help, feel free to post that link IN the original thread, so long that it’s not a personal business/ affiliate link. - If there is an important homeschool related news article, feel free to share that, but let's keep links to a minimum so conversation is not lost. Extra/excess links will be deleted without warning. -All posts concerning buying, selling or trading whether original posts or threads will be deleted. This is NOT a Buy/Sell/Trade Board. We have a Fun-Schooling B/S/T group right here —&gt;&gt; https://facebook.com/groups/FunschoolersExchange -No Soliciting. This includes essential oils, books, skincare, etc. -No Adding People From Your Friends List - They must request on their own. -No posting giveaways without permission from Admins -No blocking Admins or you will be removed from the group. -No political related posts / discussion in this group or affiliated Fun-schooling groups. -Ambassadors help answer questions, mentor and encourage mamas in the group. They have badges which indicate they are ambassadors. If you want to learn more about how to Flip to Fun-Schooling click here: http://funschoolingbooks.com/index.php?action=steps Check out some of our other affiliated groups in this file... https://www.facebook.com/notes/fun-schooling-with-thinking-tree-books/affiliated-fun-schooling-dyslexia-games-groups/2572572666356304/

                 北美菜鳥爸媽上學去-僅限「你的」+「人類」小孩4歲以上才能申請
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 申請社團請務必回答螢幕顯示的問題。沒有回答者管理員也沒有空閒審核直接拒絕。 請直接回答問題，不需再私訊管理員~~ 申請入團基本要求: 1. 您必須居住在美國、加拿大地區 2. 您必須有4歲以上已經入學的小孩 3. 您的臉書要能證明以上二個條件，如果不行，請私訊。.... 4. 有教育背景的爸媽不在此限，請私訊~ 5. 您的大頭貼不能是空白. 這是一個專為美國第一代移民父母所設立的社團。僅接受住在北美地區、家裡有上學的小孩的父母申請。還在懷孕或是小孩很小的，請申請幼兒相關社團。 第一代移民，沒有在美國成長的經驗來對應孩子的成長，所以對於學校老師的作業、Project、老師寫給家長的信，常常處於一種看的懂，卻不知所以然的狀態。 在這裡，老師出招，大家一起接招，問題可以小到school supplies的名詞看不懂，也可以複雜到Project的手工製作、材料如何運用，甚至跪求成品二手交換。總之，這裡是一個大家互相合作、一樣老鳥帶菜鳥的園地。

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Keep Calm and Homeschool On (with Jesus)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome! My name is Rebecca from homeschoolon.com and gatherroundhomeschool.com. This group is a bit different than most, so read the statement below to see if you want to be apart! It is about accountability and motivation and encouragement to walk the calling that God has given you. STATEMENT OF FAITH: Holy Spirit will be welcome in this group. It is a place where God reigns and I hereby publicly give this group to Him. We will hereinafter aim to give Him the glory in our posts, in our communication with each other, to bring unity to the body of Christ, to stand on truth and yet not judge, to be open to learning and growing in our understanding of God, and to not base our understanding of God to be based on fear or rote religion. 1. I believe the Bible to be the inspired, the only infallible, authoritative Word of God. 2. I believe that there is one God, eternally existent in three persons: Father, Son, and the Holy Spirit. Who always was, who is, and who is to come. 3. I believe that we were created in God’s image to know Him and have relationship with Him. However because we rejected Him, sickness, death, and judgement entered the world and now creation experiences the effects and consequences of sin. 4. I believe in the deity of our Lord Jesus Christ, in His virgin birth, in His sinless life, in His miracles, in His vicarious and atoning death through His shed blood, in His bodily resurrection, in His ascension to the right hand of the Father, and in His personal return in power and glory. I believe He was fully God who made Himself fully man. 5. We are saved by God’s grace, through faith in the person and work of Jesus Christ. Anyone can be restored to fellowship with God through repenting, believing, and receiving Jesus as their Savior and Lord. The Holy Spirit, convicts, regenerates, justifies, and adopts us as we enter the kingdom of God as His sons and daughters. It is not through works that we are saved, but through grace. 6. I believe that a life surrendered to God as Lord of our lives changes us and brings fruit in our lives. Jesus is the vine and we are the branches, we are called to be rooted to Him, to be in Him, and to have relationship with Him. (John 15) 7. I believe in the present ministry of the Holy Spirit who convicts, restores, comforts, reveals, and empowers the believer in his/her walk. I believe that God still speaks and that we are called to hear His voice and to follow His leading in our lives. I believe in the gifts of the Spirit. I believe that truth is not relative. I believe in women leading as God calls them, (obviously, I speak internationally, lead worship, and do all sorts of leadership things, and yet I still believe in submitting to my husband) so if you believe this to be heretical this is likely not the place for you. If you yearn to have a more active, intentional, and personal relationship with God in the day to day, come on in, I think you're gonna like it here!

                 Visual Math
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hi Teachers! 👉Please answer all questions and agree with group rules when requesting to join👈 This is a group of math educators helping each other reach kids who learn best through visuals and who may be juuust a little bit (or a whole lot) afraid of math. All kids can be successful in math with the right supports. That’s what this group is for. What thIs group is about: Sharing ideas and strategies for reaching and teaching kids in our classrooms. Math and teaching memes and jokes to keep us laughing are also welcome! What this group is not about: Homework help. Please search YouTube for help with your personal assignments. There are lots of math teaching resources (many free) and ideas on my blog scaffoldedmath.com. I hope it becomes a helpful resource for you! As teachers, we all have so much on our plates. Let’s make this group a place to support and encourage each other. Thank you for being here! -Shana McKay Scaffolded Math and Science

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Unschooling Special Needs
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                  If you do not answer screening questions, your request to join will be declined. If you are having problems on Android phone, please PM "Delia Tee" Profile pic is blue with the word "Admin". Please don't request to join if you only want to promote a business. We do not allow promotions. PM "Delia Tee" https://www.facebook.com/profile.php?id=100013236014672 if you are having trouble being added to the group. This is an UNSCHOOLING support group for parents and caregivers of Special Needs kids. We have found that NON-COERCIVE and RELATIONSHIP-BASED approaches work MUCH better for our kids than most mainstream methods of education and therapy. Unschooling is a TYPE of Homeschooling, but it is VERY different from the "school-at-home" approach most people are familiar with. It requires quite a paradigm shift in the parents' minds, which is called Deschooling. You may join to LEARN about Unschooling, get SUPPORT in switching to Unschooling, or SHARE your experience Unschooling your Special Needs child. We are a global group willing to go against the status quo of BOTH Education and Special Needs dogma. Being the parent of a child with extra challenges can be an isolating experience. Being an Unschooler can also be lonely since we are still a statistically small portion of Home Educators. Let's support each other!
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 FOR SPEECH AND LANGUAGE PROFESSIONALS ONLY. A place to discuss EBP provision of services in the schools only. *Parents need to seek a qualified SLP vs. asking for advice in this group.** POSTING OF CLIENT PHOTOS IN THE GROUP IS PROHIBITED. ALL PHOTOS WILL BE DELETED. BLOCKING OF ADMINS IS PROHIBITED: Violators may be removed from the group without notice. They will be readmitted after unblocking the admin at the admin's discretion. Threads NOT pertaining to school-based services will be deleted without notice. Repeated violations will result in offenders being removed from the group. Oral Motor/Tongue Tie/Myofunctional Therapy: Effective 4/21/17, all posts asking questions and posting unsupported opinions about oral motor exercises, tongue ties as well as oro-myofunctional therapy will be turned off and may be subject to deletion as they are NOT supported in the schools due to lack of reputable research. School-based SLPs are expected to follow their state's eligibility criteria. As per ASHA: “The decision to clip the frenulum is a medical decision made by physicians and is not in the scope of practice for speech-language pathologists." ** Effective 9/2/17, please do not ask members whether your student qualifies for therapy services based on their testing scores. Please consult your state eligibility guidelines and discuss this with your CST members. **Effective 06-04-2015, please do not ask members to provide any testing scores. All posts requesting scores will be deleted without further notice. Repeat offenders will be banned from the group without notice. ASHA's position statement link: http://community.asha.org/communities/community-home/digestviewer/viewthread?GroupId=121&amp;MID=100905&amp;tab=digestviewer ---Dear undergraduate &amp; graduate SLP students, you are gladly welcome. But please do not request help on school work/ case studies. When posting questions in this group please clearly state at the beginning of your post that you are an SLP student. --Spammers will be banned from the group. --All ads should be posted in the pinned post at the too of the page. -TPT ADVERTISERS: Limit to 5 comments per day AND restricted to direct requests /questions of members. --Admins make every attempt to ensure that all members are SLPs. However FB privacy settings can make this difficult. Please be careful of what you say. --Any advice and suggestions given in this forum are absolutely no substitute for an in person assessment by a qualified/licensed SLP. --Do not violate copyright by posting copyrighted files. They will be deleted without notice. Thanks to everyone for making this a wonderful, supportive group! 
                </div>

                 The official group for the International and Exchange Students Society at the University of Edinburgh (formerly the International Students Center Edinburgh and Exchange 360). The purpose of the this group fostering a community of current and former international students of the University of Edinburgh. ************HOUSE RULES************ This is a space for people to ask for advice, gather recommendations, and facilitate connections relating to facets of school life, living in Edinburgh, and beyond! As a result, admin reserves the right to deny the publication of the following: - Club nights ads. Even if it’s culture- or international-themed, don’t do it! We will not approve them. If you are a University of Edinburgh society looking to promote, please contact us first! - Buy or sell ads. We love recycling, but please refer to other spaces like Edinburgh - Food or items sharing (for the most part)! We are big fans of the work of the Shrub and Meadows share, so we’ll leave it to them! - Flat hunt or promotion. There are plenty of dedicated FB groups, such as Edinroom! - Proofreading freelancing or similar services. If you’re looking for proofreading, check out the great programs offered by the Student Association and the University. - Along with Facebook’s guidelines for appropriate content and the University of Edinburgh’s student code of conduct, we reserve the right to not permit posts that we deem inflammatory or derogatory, or in direct competition with the International Student Centre’s provided services, as well as removing members who do not comply to these rules. - Finally, we are not a bucket for your spam. Please don’t try and post the same thing too many times! At the end of the day, please remember to respect each other and this space (no antagonizing or harassment will be tolerated). This is a space for us to all share, learn, and get to know each other!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Preschool Teachers' Network
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 **This is the place for early childhood educators to come together, ask questions, share ideas, have fun, collaborate, and problem solve. Just like a virtual teachers' lounge! ** PLEASE READ THE GROUP RULES BEFORE POSTING. They are linked in the pinned post at the top of the group. Thank you!! We all teach in a different setting so what may work for you may not work for someone else. Be respectful, have an open mind, and keep things positive. 1. All posts and questions must be related to the education of children AGES 2-5. 2. This is not the place for self-promotion. Do not post links to products, sales promotions, social media follow threads, Donors Choose (or similar) requests, etc. Please do not share from your own business/preschool/blog pages (only admins may do so). Do not ask the other members if they want to purchase your products, etc. 3. This is a huge, international group. Do not post job listings or local events. 4. Feel free to post links that are relevant to questions and discussion. No screenshots! Absolutely no copyrighted materials may be added to the group. 5. Please keep this a supportive and kind place to be! All comments about students, parents, and other teachers must be kept professional. Keep any disagreements with other members on that same scale. In general, do not say anything in this group that you would not want printed in the newspaper. 6. No requests for homework help!! Facebook groups are not a substitute for studying and research. 7. The Admins reserve the right to delete any post that does not follow the guidelines, and to remove any member who continues to disregard them. 8. Do not request other members’ emails, and do not ask other members to PM you. 9. All posts and replies need to be in English.

                 Early Childhood Education - Early Tinkering
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome Early Tinkering enthusiasts! We're so pleased you have joined us! This group is dedicated to improving our practice, learning from each other, sharing our experiences, and promoting tinkering and making adventures with young children. Come one, come all - early childhood educators, parents, early childhood caregivers, school administrators, tinker and maker experts and experimenters, museum educators, and other joyful tinkerers who work with little minds! We CELEBRATE the creative learning process in ourselves, as well as in the little people in our lives. We embrace the process of dreaming, designing, experimenting, practicing, failing, iterating...many, many times. Together we hope to increase our abilities to nurture the 21st century skills of critical thinking, creativity, collaboration, communication in ourselves and in the very young people in our lives. #earlytinkering - We started this hashtag on Instagram. Please use it there as another way to share your practice.

                 Abraham Lincoln High School Alumni - Los Angeles, CA
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Established in 1878, Abraham Lincoln High School in Los Angeles, CA nurtured and kindled countless minds of young adults growing up around the Lincoln Heights area. All graduates and alumni of Abraham Lincoln High School (LAUSD) are welcomed to join. Please feel free to make use of this group to keep in contact with your former classmates, update your friends about reunions, or meet up with your old high school sweethearts... On Wikipedia: http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abraham_Lincoln_High_School_%28Los_Angeles%2C_California%29 ~~~~~~~~~~ School Information: Year Opened: 1878 Colours: Black and Orange Mascot: Tiger Alma Mater: "All Hail To Lincoln" Words by Agnes E. Peterson Music by Louis W. Curtis All hail! All hail! To Lincoln hail! Hail alma mater true! Throned on thy heights that upward reach, To skies of cloudless blue. Our hearts beat warm in loyalty, Our love shall never fail; To thee, in praise our song we raise, All hail, to Lincoln, hail! Hail, alma mater, Lincoln, hail! Thy loyal sons so bold shall count their duty but a joy thy honor to uphold. Untarnished shall thy fair name shine, No doubts thy fame assail; Each heart and voice approve our choice, All hail, to Lincoln, hail! When, alma mater, far from thee Our wand'ring paths shall turn, Still for thy ever fost'ring care Thy children all shall yearn. Thy kindly lore, thy creed so true, Within us shall prev'l; And then each heart shall own thy party, All hail, to Lincoln, hail! ~~~~~~~~~~ Disclaimer: This "Abraham Lincoln High School Alumni - Los Angeles, CA" Facebook group is not in any way affiliated with the "Lincoln Alumni Association" or endorsed by them. You are NOT required to pay membership fees/dues to join or to continue membership in THIS Facebook group. We do not claim to be the "official" alumni association for Abraham Lincoln High School. This group was created for persons interested in connecting with Lincoln alumni over Facebook. (Updated: 06 February, 2009) ~~~~~~~~~~ Go Tigers!

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Affording the Homeschool Life
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Affording the Homeschool Life is a group for homeschool families to share tips, tricks, and resources for all frugal living topics. Feel free to post questions and please join in the conversation! You'll also find daily homeschool freebies, deals, and articles from FreeHomeschoolDeals.com. Let's keep this group fun and encouraging! The owner and admin of this group is Free Homeschool Deals | Homeschool Solutions, LLC. Community Guidelines: *Affiliate links and spam will be removed.* Please do not post fundraising requests in this group. I'm unable to monitor these with a group of this size. This includes, but not limited to, GoFundMe links, Kickstarter, YouCaring, etc. Drama &amp; KINDNESS Guidelines: Please be kind to one another and respectful. There are families from all walks of life in this group. As this group continues to grow there are sometimes posts or comments that start controversy and drama. Our admins and moderators will do their best to monitor and vet each post as it comes through. However, if there is a post that we receive multiple complaints over, for the sake of time and sanity, we will delete the post in question. HOT TOPICS: All people are welcome in this group. Posts about "hot topics" such as religion and politics quickly get out of hand. Those posts may be deleted at the discretion of the admins. If repeated offenses occur by the same poster, they will be removed from the group. BLOGGERS: I know there are lots of bloggers in this group and we all love to share. This isn't a place to share your blog posts each day. Also, do not share any direct affiliate links in this group. However, using good judgement, you may share what you have written or created that is relevant to this group if you can share in a natural way within the comments. Posts that are just dropped in the group will be deleted. NO FILE SHARING: Due to many, many, copyright rules this is just a reminder to please not upload or share files in this group that YOU did not create. Even if it's a "freebie," we still can't directly share a file in this group. The creators of these files get paid, if you will, by web traffic to where their freebies are located. They do not give permission for the actual file to be spread around the web freely. You can certainly share a web address location as to where the freebie can be found, but not the actual file usually ending in .pdf. We want to keep this group as a resourceful encouragement to all homeschool families. *If you feel any other guidelines need to be added to this group, or have any additional questions, please email us at: contact@freehomeschooldeals.com
                </div>

                 Special Education Teachers
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group was created by the National Association of Special Education Teachers as a place for #SpecialEducation Teachers to assist each other with best practices and tips. The rules of this community are simple. First, your posts and comments must add value. Posts with links, videos, or pictures must also include meaningful comments within the posts themselves that add value. Maintain confidentiality of your students. Be courteous and encouraging to your colleagues in the group. Use appropriate and professional language. Stay on topic, special education. Posts with links to promotions or spam, rudeness, irrelevance or repetitive in nature will be deleted. Not observing these simple rules will get you banned. *UPDATE* 8/7: NASET wants to keep the discussions posted in this Special Education Group about special education, and all posts &amp; sharing that appear political or are primarily addressing political issues regardless of the political leaning will be deleted. Those who place these types of posts may face removal from the group. Thanks for joining us! www.naset.org #SpecialEducationTeachers

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Homeschooling Dyslexic Kids
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is a support group for homeschool families where we can be free to speak our heart and mind on the subject of dyslexia and our children. Please be considerate of one another. We are here to lift one another up and help to lighten the load of others just starting out. I know it's a fine line for some of our moms who are also therapist/tutors and we appreciate that you are here as a mom first. Remember ladies that this group is for Homeschool moms and dads. I realize that everyone has their favorite OG curriculum that they love, just keep in mind that there are others on the market that also work and not everyone will agree with you. Please do not put added pressure on those who choose (for whatever reason) to use something else. Comments like "don't waste your money", "all I use in my private practice" or "don't you care about your child's future" will be removed as they are not helpful to the group. I know that all your hearts are in the right place, but I get PM's from a lot of mom's saying that these kinds of comments make them feel inadequate or like failures if they can’t afford some of the higher priced products. It's okay to say you "highly recommend whatever" but don't knock other forms of remediation, that may be all the person is able to use, It is okay to share therapies and services/websites as long as it directly relates to home-school or dyslexia. Do Not PM other members of this group unless you are asked to. This will get you removed from the group. If you are asked to then, by all means, go ahead. You can sell items or curriculum as long as they are home-school or dyslexia-related, but these transactions will be between buyer and seller only and to be handled via PM and not on the page. This is NOT a page to solicit business of any kind that includes but not limited to (ie. tutoring/therapy services, books, gadgets, sunglasses, boots or direct-sales business, or PMing member to offer services, etc). There are many other pages for growing your business and this is not it. If this happens you will be removed. EDIT: We do allow all business owners (homeschool and therapist/tutors or online learning academies or webpages) to share your business on the First Monday of the month ONLY! We do want to help our working mom's but we must keep this support group Dyslexia focused. No affiliate links are allowed except by our admins. We DO NOT discuss religion or politics but we will allow you to ask for prayer. If you are not religious then scroll on by. Below are some sites to get you started on your journey. We are glad you found us and welcome to the group. Your Admin Team. http://www.dys-add.com/ http://dyslexia.yale.edu/About_ShaywitzBios.htmlhttp://homeschoolingwithdyslexia.com/
                </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Global Educator Collective
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to our Educator Collective. We are a group of educators from all over the world sharing our expertise and supporting one another. We seek to empower educators as effective leaders of learning within their contexts. Mission: Maintain a global platform for continuous educator development with intent to inspire authentic, purposeful learning and learner agency. The objective of Global Educator Collective is to contribute to educator development through collaborative learning shared in best practices, pedagogy, shared resources, strategies, experiences and perspectives through a safe environment that builds understanding. This is still a very new group which formed out of crisis. The current administrators and moderators are simply people who stepped up in a time of crisis. The world is in a time of rapid change and evolution. This group reflects that. We want to diversify the leadership of our group and we also need more volunteers from diverse backgrounds. Volunteers in this group are full time educators whose first duty is to their own family and health, and secondly to their schools and students. In their spare time, they carry out a range of roles and tasks in the group and contribute in many ways. We respect that this group may not be for everyone and we understand that there are multiple perspectives. Read our rules and please be open minded to learn from others and also interact positively and constructively. 
                </div>

                 Christian Homeschool Families
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group was founded for the purpose of encouraging and assisting Christian families to home educate with a Biblical worldview according to God's clear instructions to do so. This includes those who are already homeschooling, those who plan to homeschool, and those who are wisely concerned about the government schools and who are seeking a Christian alternative. The Bible is the inerrant and infallible Word of God, and the source of all truth. We ask that all posts and discussions be based upon this irrefutable fact. Feel free to share, encourage, and ask questions. 3 John 1:4 "I have no greater joy than to hear that my children walk in truth." Rules: 1. Be Christ-like and judge all things rightly. 2. There is no profanity allowed. 3. Spam will be promptly deleted. Please no soliciting or marketing for personal gain including the selling of curriculum. If you have any questions, please send a private message to one of the administrators. 4. This group does not support the government schools or their unBiblical teachings. This group is for those home educating, those who are considering doing so, and those who have the sincere desire to learn more about the blessings of home education. We will not tolerate anyone misrepresenting themselves in an effort to undermine Christian education. 5. Please read the pinned post that clarifies the group's rules.

                 AIESEC WHOLE WORLD
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Present in over 127 countries and territories and with over 60,000 members, AIESEC is the world's largest student‐run organisation. Focused on providing a platform for youth leadership development, AIESEC offers young people the opportunity to be global citizens, to change the world, and to get experience and skills that matter today. AIESEC is the international platform for young people to explore and develop their leadership potential so as to have a positive impact on society. AIESEC International cooperates with a select group of organizations on programs and activities with a global reach. AIESEC Alumni (ex-members) are located all over the globe, working in various professions and industries and playing important roles in their communities. Visit our website to see more of our stories and what you can do as a member/partner/alumni of AIESEC. Visit www.aiesec.org to contact AIESEC near you! --------------- This virtual group is intended for current and previous members of AIESEC (Alumni). Please share information about current programs,&amp;nbsp; activities and opportunities related to the Association. Job posting and educational issues are also OK.&lt;br&gt; If you have been rejected from joining this group and you are or have been a member of AIESEC in an LC, MC, AI or another entity, please email info@ai.aiesec.org with your date of joining AIESEC, the LC you joined with and myAIESEC.net logon ID so we can double check our records. Presente en más de 127 países y territorios y con más de 60.000 miembros, AIESEC es la organización dirigida por estudiantes más grande del mundo. Enfocada en proporcionar una plataforma para el desarrollo del liderazgo juvenil, AIESEC ofrece a los jóvenes la oportunidad de ser ciudadanos globales, de cambiar el mundo y de adquirir experiencia y habilidades que hoy importan. AIESEC es la plataforma internacional para que los jóvenes exploren y desarrollen su potencial de liderazgo para tener un impacto positivo en la sociedad. AIESEC Internacional coopera con un selecto grupo de organizaciones en programas y actividades de alcance mundial. Los ex alumnos de AIESEC (ex-miembros) están ubicados en todo el mundo, trabajando en diversas profesiones e industrias y desempeñando papeles importantes en sus comunidades. Visite www.aiesec.org para comunicarse con AIESEC cerca de usted. --------------- Este grupo virtual está dirigido a miembros actuales y anteriores de AIESEC (Alumni). Comparte información sobre los programas actuales; &amp; nbsp; actividades y oportunidades relacionadas con la Asociación. Las postulaciones para empleo y los temas educativos también se permiten. Si usted ha sido rechazado de unirse a este grupo y es o ha sido miembro de AIESEC en una LC, MC, AI u otra entidad, por favor envíe un correo electrónico a info@ai.aiesec.org con su fecha de adhesión a AIESEC, el LC con el cual se unió y myAIESEC.net ID de inicio de sesión para que podamos comprobar nuestros registros.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 NOTE: If you Request to join - be sure to answer the three questions that Facebook prompts you to. Please read the whole description of this group to see if you are eligible to join. Homeschooling in Southern California is a Group that provides information about homeschooling specific to Southern California. Group members are welcome to share links, classes, ideas, inspirations and events. We welcome both active and prospective homeschoolers. We do not allow spam. But we welcome those who have related businesses that homeschoolers might be interested in. We ask that vendors and charter schools advertise their business or event no more than two times per month. You may group events together into one post if you have several. Please realize that our members have vastly diverse homeschooling methods, religious and socio-political beliefs, come from different economic backgrounds, races, religions and have vastly different parenting methods. Ensure that anything you post is helpful, respectful and kind. We have a "scroll past" rule. If you come across a posting that you would never utilize for your children, scroll past. Be supportive, or scroll past. If you are looking for general information about homeschooling in California, it's legalities and how to get started, please visit either of our three statewide organizations, California Homeschool Network http://www.californiahomeschool.net/ or Homeschool Association of California https://www.hsc.org/ or Christian Home Educators of California http://www.cheaofca.org/

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Montessori Homeschooling
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 YOU ARE REQUIRED TO ANSWER THE THREE MEMBERSHIP REQUEST QUESTIONS IN A SATISFACTORY MANNER TO HAVE MEMBERSHIP APPROVED. Montessori Homeschooling is a support group for home educating families who wish to incorporate the Montessori Method. We encompasses individuals who are working with school-age children in primary, elementary, and beyond (age 3 through graduation). Our group includes a wide range of experience from those who are looking for more information to accredited Montessori teachers. Our members also incorporate Montessori in various ways and at different degrees. We ask that all participants be respectful of each other. Montessori strives for peace - teaching children to be tolerant of others and refraining from hateful words. Those same expectations are found here. By requesting to join this group, you agree to the following: 1 - All posts should be relevant to using the Montessori Method and/or home schooling for school aged children. 2 - You may post a non-commercial link to your blog, website, or FB page once per week, provided you are an active member. You may post links in replies, provided they are relevant to the topic being discussed. 3 – Businesses may post about a relevant product or service offered with a limit of one post per month, provided they are an active member (contributing meaningfully on other discussions). You may not advertise on other threads. Due to the size of our group, consultants from MLMs are not permitted to advertise. 4 – No self-promotion, including votes for contests, the solicitation of money, affiliate links, or promotion of other groups/campaigns. You many not solicit members via PM. 5 – Name calling, division, or other hateful behavior will not be tolerated. 6 – You may not post pictures of children that are not your own nor may you share things posted in this group elsewhere. 7 – We are not equipped to handle buying and selling in this group. Please see https://www.facebook.com/groups/MontessoriMaterialForSale/ 8 – Be respectful of the individual journey each family is on. It is not acceptable to berate individuals who chose another path on controversial topics. As a support group, we take a “No Drama” stance. Do not bring issues from other groups to this one. Posts not meeting our guidelines will be removed without warning. Serious or repeat offenders will be banned without notice. If you have an issue with a post, tag our admins: Group Owner/Admin - Bess Wuertz You can also send a PM.

                 ยินดีต้อนรับสู่กลุ่ม Study, Work, and Family Support for Thais in America ค่ะ บ้านนี้สร้างขึ้นเพื่อให้ความรู้และช่วยเหลือใน 3หัวข้อหลักๆ คือเรื่องเรียน การทำงาน และ ปัญหาครอบครัว ของคนไทย ในอเมริกา เท่านั้น กรุณาอ่านกฏนะคะ เพราะทีมแอดมินเข้มมาก โพสต์ผิดกฏจะถูกลบทันทีค่ะ 1) เรื่องเรียน ปัญหาการเรียน การสมัครเรียน ทุกระดับชั้น ในอเมริกาเท่านั้น ยินดีให้คำปรึกษา สำหรับคนที่อยู่ไทย ที่กำลังวางแผนมาเรียนที่อเมริกาค่ะ 2) การทำงานทุกอาชีพที่สุจริต ในอเมริกาเท่านั้น 3) ปัญหาครอบครัว การปรับตัวสำหรับคนมาอยู่ใหม่ ปัญหาความรุนแรงในครอบครัว mental health, social work, ถ้ามีปัญหาครอบครัว ถูกทำร้าย เราหาข้อมูลให้ได้ *********ข้อห้าม********** *** งดโพสต์ดราม่า สร้างความแตกแยก หมิ่นเบื้องสูง ชาติ ศาสนา พระมหากษัตริย์ *** งดโพสต์ขายของ เรี่ยไรเงิน หรือรับบริจาค ทุกชนิด สำหรับผู้ที่มีความเดือดร้อนทางปัญหาครอบครัว เรายินดีให้คำปรึกษาเพื่อแก้ไขค่ะ แต่ไม่ให้มีการมาขอเรี่ยไรเงินค่ะ และขอร้อง อย่าตีหน้าเศร้าเล่าความเท็จ ไม่เอานะคะ *** งดโพสต์ปัญหาสัพเพเหระ ที่ไม่ใช่ 3หัวข้อสำคัญข้างต้น มีหลายกลุ่มที่สร้างขึ้นเพื่อรองรับสาระพันปัญหาอยู่แล้ว กรุณาโพสต์ให้ถูกที่ค่ะ เราต้องการสร้างจุดยืนให้กลุ่มนี้ ให้เป็นกลุ่มเฉพาะจริงๆค่ะ *** ไม่รับปรึกษาปัญหา วีซ่า กรีนการ์ด หรือซิติเซ่นชิพค่ะ วีซ่าทำงานหรือวีซ่านักเรียนก็ไม่ได้ค่ะ รบกวนสอบถามที่กลุ่มวีซ่านะคะ

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Preschool Printables
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Anyone interested in preschool printable activities is welcome to join! The mission of this group is simple: to share links to our favorite free and paid preschool printables from around the web! The rules for this group are simple too! Who can post? Group admins and moderators may post in this group. I have invited some of my favorite printable creators to share links to their best printable creations with all of you! What can moderators post? As a moderator, you may post links to as many of your own free printables as you wish. You may post a link to one of your own paid printable products once a week. All printables must be suitable for the preschool-kindergarten age range. Please do not post links to blog posts that are not about printables. Only our founding members (who joined prior to October 2017) have permission to post multiple paid products per week, including affiliate links. What else can moderators do? Share links to your own printables and feel free to invite anyone you wish to join the group! Please do not add others as moderators, or approve others' posts, or add links to non-printable related blog posts. You are encouraged to spread the word about this group to your own audiences. The larger the group, the more we all benefit! What can general members do? Feel free to comment on any of the links and ask questions about the printables. Invite your friends to join this group! What makes this group unique? The links shared here are directly from the printable creators themselves so you can trust they're not stolen or violating anyone's copyright! We hope you enjoy using these awesome printables with your preschoolers! Thanks again for joining us, and a VERY special thank you to the group moderators for sharing their talents with us!

                 STEAM Kids: Fun, Hands-On Learning Activities for Kids
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Fun, hands-on Science, Technology, Engineering, Art, &amp; Math activities for kids ages 4-12. This is a place to find ideas, ask questions and discuss STEM &amp; STEAM education. PLEASE READ THE GROUP RULES BEFORE POSTING. Thank you!! 1. IT'S ALL ABOUT STEAM: All posts and questions must be related to STEAM (science, technology, engineering, art, and math) education and activities. 2. PLEASE POST COOL STUFF! Feel free to post links that are relevant to questions and discussion from your own site or elsewhere. We love learning from all. 3. NO SELF-PROMOTION OR SPAM: This is not the place for self-promotion. Do not post links to products, referral links, sales promotions, social media follow threads, events, Donors Choose (or similar) requests, etc. 4. DON'T ASK FOR FOLLOWS: Do not post requests for follows or likes for your own social media, blogs, videos, etc. 5. ADMINS ARE HERE TO HELP: The Admins reserve the right to delete any post that does not follow the guidelines, and to remove any member who continues to disregard them. See something that looks out of place? Please report it and we’ll take care of it. Thanks so much for joining us in the STEAM Kids: Fun, Hands-on Learning Activities for Kids group!

                 There are 2 Admins for this group, please direct any questions/concerns to us in a private message Admin/ Owner of the Group - Trish Corlew Admin Leann Warren RULES: 1.) Any Montessori school or homeschool items may be posted. (Businesses can only advertise once per month). Please only use your own pictures (no stock images). 2.) All costs must be agreed upon by both parties prior to payments. 3.) Once your item has been sold, and the buyer has received the item, please delete it so it doesn't clog up the board. 4.) You may bump your unsold items once every 24 hours. But if it has not sold in a week. Please do not continue to bump the item every day. At most once per week after the first week. 5.) We are a group of people with the same goal...providing a good education for our children ...any insulting, inappropriate, racist, or in any way offensive comments will be deleted and the offending person will be banned from the group. 6.) All transactions are between the seller and the buyer. Disputes will not be settled by the administrators of this group. To protect both the buyer and seller, we recommend PayPal be used. Do NOT use "send money to friend / family". If you do, you lose your ability to dispute the transaction. Seller cannot add an additional fee to the transaction either. 7.) Sellers please go in order of who responded first (not the first to say SOLD. If a buyer is asking questions, they are in line first). Please give a reasonable amount of time to respond (usually 24 hours). Buyers, please do not PM the seller with your interest in an item. It makes it very difficult for the sellers to keep up with who is first in line. Therefore, only the comments on the posts will be considered as "the legitimate line". 8.) Feel free to add your friends... but ask them to read this information :-) 9.) Administrators reserve the right to delete any posts that are not related to Montessori or homeschooling. 10.) New International sellers.We ask that you only list three items initially. Once you have successful transactions with happy buyers, we will release you from the selling limitation. 11.) No affiliate links. The owner of this group will post deals she finds that will include an affiliate link. No other affiliate links are allowed. 12.) If you are looking for an item, start your post with "ISO" (In search of). 13.) Do NOT solicit for any type of business, no exceptions.And do not PM our members with unsolicited information. 14.) NO SPAM! This includes, but is not limited to, "join my team" type posts, anything asking for donations in money form, any product/service/ opportunity that claims "no money up front". Spamming will NOT be tolerated 15.) NO PORNOGRAPHIC MATERIAL OF ANY KIND! 16.) Books have been moved to our sister group, https://www.facebook.com/groups/UsedChildrensBooks/. Only Montessori Manuals and books can be sold here in this group. 17.) Do not block the admin. 
                </div>

                 Please remember that this group was created by The Primary Gal to give special education teachers ideas, support, and inspiration. 🎉 This is not a group for promoting your own businesses, resources or websites. Please do not: -start a post to share your own blog post or products (free or paid) -start a post that is a picture of your product -share affiliate links -share your Donor's Choose projects unless admin starts a thread -go live in the group without admin approval -post things that are not teaching related -complain about the teaching profession *Group administrator is excluded and may share links to relevant and helpful posts and resources.

                 Modern Preschool Teachers &amp; Parents
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the Modern Preschool Parents &amp; Teachers FB group! This group is for parents, teachers, grandparents, childcare workers...really anyone who loves keeping kids (babies, toddlers, preschoolers, &amp; school-aged kids) busy with Modern Preschool activities! We've all been there...sometimes you're on a roll with great ideas, sometimes you need an accountability partner to keep going, and sometimes you just need some new inspiration. ----&gt; Now you have a place to share ideas, ask questions, support others, chat about what's going on with your favorite kiddos, and make friends! The things this group is NOT about: *selling preschool (or other) products or self-promoting your own website, TpT account, or other unrelated products (make-up, facial care, leggings, etc.) *inquiring about jobs, member emails, donations, or messaging any members privately to sell or request anything from them Admin members reserve the right to remove members, photos, comments, threads at any time for not following group guidelines. Where to start? 1. Find, comment, and read about other members here: https://www.facebook.com/groups/ModernPreschool/permalink/954869454629933/ 2. Look around! Check out different threads posted for fun ideas, or maybe to help answer a question that was asked. 3. Give us a peek at your week! Start your own thread with a question, share an activity (photo or description), or with a new idea you've tried! 4. Have fun and be interactive! You'll get the most out of the group this way! Can't wait to get to know you all better! ~ Nicole (mom, teacher, &amp; creator of Modern Preschool) PS...this is not a group for negativity. There is enough of that floating around Facebook on a daily basis - this is a place to build each other up!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to our own space on Facebook to buy, sell, and swap *curriculum*. By requesting/accepting membership you are agreeing to follow all group rules so please take the time to read the pinned post, FAQ file, &amp; Paypal, shipping, &amp; packaging file upon approval. This is an international group, but the vast majority of members are in the US. Please keep this in mind. Not all sellers are willing to ship outside the US &amp; it is not required. If you're outside the US you should not expect PPD prices to apply &amp; should inform the other party of your location before an exchange of funds. Pinned Post: https://www.facebook.com/groups/Homeschool.Curriulum.Marketplace/permalink/1064215463590046/ FAQ: https://www.facebook.com/notes/homeschool-curriculum-marketplace/faqs/1064072790270980 Paypal, Shipping, &amp; Packaging 101: https://www.facebook.com/notes/homeschool-curriculum-marketplace/paypal-shipping-packaging-101/860551643956430 Rule summary: -Curriculum only, no toys, clothes, household, etc -All posts, even ISO, must be in sell something format -All sale posts must include photos/descriptions/prices &amp; must be available to ship at time of posting -Delete posts once payment is received, marking sold does NOT delete -Bumping is allowed every 7 days, no more than 10 posts/day -Report all issues to admin, no transaction complaints on the wall -NO discussion posts, we are for sales only -NO “friends &amp; family” Paypal -NO external links -NO businesses/advertising or digital only products -NO albums, events, videos, or files -NO blocking admin -NO hijacking posts Details on rules are in the pinned post. Admin are not responsible for transactions that take place on this group. We will however investigate complaints to the best of our ability &amp; remove members when we see fit.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 ADayInOurShoes.com -- IEP assistance, support, parenting &amp; more
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Please read before you ask to join: This is only for families who are eligible for an IEP--USA, American territories, American military bases overseas. This is a place for special needs parents to connect for IEP advice, special needs parenting tips and more. This group is an off-shoot of my blog ADayInOurShoes.com. This is a group for those who have a vested interest in the special needs community and wish to be kept informed about policies and legislation that affect our kids, and act upon it by contacting our legislators. If you were not approved, read this: https://www.freelancerstools.com/rules-for-running-facebook-group/ Please look here to see if your question is answered, including looking for an advocate: https://adayinourshoes.com/iep-meeting-advice-parents/ Please do a search (on left hand side) before asking your question, and feel free to add to that thread or bump it up. We get a large amount of duplicate questions. Please refrain from giving or asking for medical advice (including Rx), using words like legal/illegal/sue/against the law, as we do not allow medical or legal advice in here. Vaccine chat is discouraged and usually deleted (because it always goes negative!) as are most threads talking about cures or alternative treatments. Let the buyer beware: it is the internet. We try to correct misinformation when we see it, but we don't see it all. Always double check before proceeding. Refrain from posting information that is not requested. This group is mainly for parents to ask questions and get advice on handling situations. If you have a link that is helpful, post it as a response. There is a monthly thread where you can post links to articles, videos and even your own website or fundraiser. It is pinned to the top of the group and changes monthly. Reasons your post may have been deleted: • Pictures/videos of children • Recommending advice that is against the law/IDEA • You posted another thread saying, “hey why was it deleted?” • The thread spiraled out of control (or was headed that way) into a cesspool of negativity or extremely off topic • giving medical advice It is Facebook and no one should assume 100% privacy. Solicitation is not allowed. Do not start more than 1 thread per day. I may include some of your questions as part of the Q&amp;A I do on my blog, as a resource for other parents. I NEVER use names, school districts or any other personal information. I try to remain laid back and positive, as do the other admins. However, my name and website and business name is attached to this, so I take it seriously.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Radical Unschooling
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome! This group was started in 2012. Radical Unschooling and Unschooling are two different philosophies. Unschooling is living without school and trusting your children with their education. Radical Unschooling is trusting your children in *every* area of their lives, not just education. Another way it can be described is Radical Unschooling is living in a partnership paradigm of parenting, as opposed to the traditional authoritarian paradigm. One can Unschool education, but still live in the authoritarian paradigm, but that isn't Radical Unschooling. PLEASE READ THESE Group Guidelines: No topics or comments against Radical Unschooling philosophy/principles or articles promoting child abuse through promoting punishments. They will be deleted. Flaming admin. and other members is not welcome. (ie name calling and stirring.) Obviously, a troll will get through from time to time. Please notify admin's if you notice trolly activities. Flouncing isn't welcome. If you'd like to leave the group, please do so, but please be respectful about it. We ask that you do not post venting or complaining about non-RU parenting practices. We'd like to promote what we are for, not focus on what we are against, as much as possible. If you enter a debate make sure you can handle debates that cat get heated. Please stay respectful and practice peaceful communication to the best of your ability. Please, no spin off threads starting conflict or cross posting arguments. If you have a problem with another member, contact admins or pm that person you have a problem with. Do not make the issue public on the group . No screen shots from this group are to be taken and posted anywhere else. This is a safe place what happen here, stays here. Instant ban for people doing this. If you see posts from this group posted else where please pm admin.. People who are uncivil and abusive will be removed. Please be respectful to all members. Everyone is on a different place in their journey. It is important to be supportive. Extending Radical Unschooling philosophy to everyone in your life is an art. Please practice it here and learn from others who do. . Peace &amp; Love, Dayna Martin website: www.daynamartin.com email: officialdaynamartin@yahoo.com mail: Dayna Martin 196 East Madison Rd. Madison, NH 03849 USA For speaking inquires or to inquire about one on one parenting coaching, please visit my website.

We may collect your email as while asking to Join the Group and added to Newsletter from Happy Schools (that you can unsubscribe anytime). 3. No blatant advertising or marketing allowed. Anyone who drops in out of nowhere and posts an advertisement to the community may be removed at the discretion of the Community Admins. If you want to promote, reach out to Admin's. 4. At all times be authentic, honest, act in good faith, and post-high-value high content and solutions. Do your best to build a strong reputation, provide actionable insight, and keep it inside the group. 5. We hate fake profiles! If we find one (from comments, posts, new members request), we may Block the Account from this group (and other related groups of Happy Schools). 6. Search for solutions before posting your questions. And Read the Comments for Valuable Insights and Answers. 7. You retain the rights to your work, except that your contributions may be re-purposed and redistributed. You grant Happy Schools a perpetual license to republish the material at its sole discretion. 8. Before you publish a post, take the time to proof and edit. Remember, you are being published and your participation paints a picture of your character to other members of the group. 9. Please don't use special characters to follow the post (like F, Follow, #, Following). Instead, Turn on Post Notifications. 10. Please don't TAG the Admins, Moderators, Attorney's to get answers to your questions. 11. We often get "Sorry, I didn't know the polices", will not get you back into the group once an account is removed. So, please, please read the guidelines and get yourself familiar with our guidelines. 12. In short - Be Good. Be Helpful or Be Gone!                  Benchmark Advance collaborative group created by Toluca Rivers from Markers and Minions. This is a place to discuss all things Benchmark Advance - across all grade levels. Disclaimer: I share what works for me &amp; my third grade class. This is NOT a group run by Benchmark Education Company. My ideas are based on my personal experiences and include teaching strategies I’ve learned outside of Benchmark. Take any idea you’d like, but don’t feel like it’s the only way to do things. 🙂 To find my Benchmark resources: http://bit.ly/2eAuLNn

                 A collective of resources and a place to share ideas with each other to support special learners, particularly during Distance Learning. Parents, educators, and therapists welcome! Membership requests must answer 1 question AND agree to the group rules before approval. Group rules: ⭐️ Protect privacy and confidentiality: No posting photos of students or names of students. ⭐️ Contribute to a solutions-oriented community: Posting frustrations and/or concerns should remain solutions-oriented and to reach out for support and encouragement. Simply venting and creating a negative environment is not allowed. ⭐️ Be Kind and Courteous: We're all in this together to create a welcoming environment. Let's treat everyone with respect. Healthy debates are natural, but kindness is required. No snark, and assume positive intent. ⭐️ No Hate Speech or Bullying: Make sure everyone feels safe. Bullying of any kind isn't allowed, and degrading comments about things like race, religion, culture, sexual orientation, gender or identity will not be tolerated. ⭐️ Limit self-promotion: You are welcomed to share materials that group members may find useful; however, please limit self promotion as well as posts related to publications for sale. ⭐️ No Spam: Spam and irrelevant links aren't allowed.

                 The Homeschool Summits group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the Homeschool Summits Facebook group! The purpose of this group is to connect Christian homeschooling families around the world to share resources and encouragement for Christ-centered home education and discipleship. Learn more about our FREE online events here at HomeschoolSummits.com. Here are our group rules: 1. Please join in with your experiences and ideas as we learn together! 2. Be respectful, positive, kind, and honoring to Christian and family-friendly values. (This is a fun, encouraging, polite platform for discussion, and negative/continually argumentative posts and members will be removed from the group.) 3. This group is for the international Christian homeschooling community. Therefore, do not share any posts or comments that are local/regional-specific, or advocate for programs, materials, or resources that are not parent-led, Christ-centered, and free from government control. 4. Promotional posts and resource links are permitted by current Homeschool Summits sponsors, partners, and exhibitors only. All other promotional or sales posts (whether shared or posted) that are not related to Homeschool Summits will be deleted. If someone else posts a question, you are welcome to reply with a comment for your recommendation of any Christian/family-friendly material. 5. Events and videos (live, pre-recorded, or shared) are only permitted by the Homeschool Summits admin or, if approved, our sponsors, partners, or exhibitors. 6. Soliciting contacts to build your business is not permitted (sending private messages, “PM me for more info,” crowdsourcing, repeatedly sharing out-of-context recommendations, etc.) 7. Violating the rules stated here may result in immediate deletion of the post without warning, and may result in a PM as a reminder of our rules and/or removal from the group. Questions or interested in partnering with Homeschool Summits as an affiliate or exhibitor? Contact Katie at katie@homeschoolsummits.com (or tag Katie Ward in a comment).

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 The Sensory Motor Classroom
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a group for all those interested in sharing sensory and motor ideas in the classroom! As a paediatric OT, my intention behind this group is to build a community that is a safe supportive space for questions, information and resources around all things sensory and motor within the classroom. I know many of you will have amazing Occupational Therapists working in your schools that give you great information for specific students. The sensory strategies and foundational motor and sensory information will apply to all students. Many of the motor and sensory activities posted here will be aimed towards students at the developmental age of 3-9 years old or those students who are older with delays in these areas. Please feel free to share relevant information and resources, ask questions, comment or simply read. Welcome to all Special Education and Mainstream Teachers, Teaching Assistants, Home School Teachers or Parents, Occupational Therapists, Occupational Therapist Assistants, Other Therapists, and School Staff. I look forward to us all sharing! Disclaimer: The resources, information, strategies and posts in the Sensory Motor Classroom are for collaboration, supplementary support and general educational purposes only. The information is not intended as a replacement for Occupational Therapy or Specialist Teaching services. Members are encouraged to reach out to their local providers and teams for individualized programmes for specific students. 
                </div>

                 This group is for buying, selling, or swapping books that relate to a Charlotte Mason, Living Book, literature based type of teaching/learning style. If I find out you are not, I will not hesitate to remove and block you. #2 Rule- ALL TRANSACTIONS ARE BETWEEN BUYER &amp; SELLER and at your own risk. Admins are not here to handle disputes. TIPS TO HELP~ USE PAYPAL it offers protection, NEVER use anything but the GOODS &amp; Services option or you lose proctection. PAYPAL fees are part of doing business, do NOT charge your buyer your Paypal fees, simply figure that into the cost along with your packing if desired. PACK WELL, make sure your items are secure and can not shift during shipping. If you have a high priced order insist on using insurance at the Post Office. I love my fellow homeschool Mamas and hope I can continue to serve you.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Google Classroom for Teachers
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for TEACHERS at all levels--elementary school to university--who are using Google Classroom. TO BE APPROVED TO JOIN THIS GROUP you must answer the automated group questions. Welcome to the Group! Updated: 7.14.2020 GROUP RULES POSTS 1—All posts must be about or related to Google Classroom (which includes the Google Suite). Posts must be in English; please translate other languages into English. 2—Include in the first line of your post: (1) grade level (all, elem school, middle school, high school, college) and (2) a topic/few words that summarize your post and would be helpful for group members, such as: Forms, Sites, Quiz, Drive, Rubrics, etc. 3—Off-topic posts will be deleted. SPAM posts will be deleted and the individual will be removed from the group. Posts about Google Certification aren't allowed. Do not post items, books, services, and workshops that you are selling. 4—Sharing a link to your own blog or page? The content you're linking to should be free, and your post must include a brief description of what you're linking to. Posting a link just to receive more clicks to your own personal site is not allowed. 5—To keep this group focused and easy to search, unrelated technology and Bitmoji posts are not allowed. Please find another group for those posts. SEARCH FIRST &amp; TOPICS Have a question? Please search previous posts using the SEARCH THIS GROUP field on the left side of your screen. Your question may already have be answered. You can also browse the group Units and Topic Tags for previous ideas answers. CONTRIBUTE &amp; COURTESY Please share your ideas, solutions and expertise. Be courteous to other group members. Remember: what works/doesn't work in your classroom may well work/not work in someone else's.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 ADHD Parents Homeschooling ADHD Kids
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for adults with ADHD who are homeschooling or actively considering homeschooling kids who also have ADHD in the immediate future. To respect member privacy, we do not admit parents who plan to homeschool sometime in the future or suspect their child may have ADHD but they are too young to make that determination. We also do not admit parents who are only temporarily using virtual school during COVID. There's a lot of support for neurotypical parents and their kids (ADHD or not), but being an ADHD parent adds a whole new layer to the beautiful chaos. We do not require an official diagnosis for yourself or your child to be a member of this group. However, this group is for the parent who actually has ADHD, not spouses without ADHD. This allows us to have a community that understands the experience personally and can openly ask for support for their kids or themselves when needed. So, this is a place where we can support each other, vent about struggles, exchange ideas, ask questions, make suggestions, and make friends! To maintain an open and safe environment, we ask that everyone respect each other’s privacy by not sharing any information outside the group.
