               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Lynwood High Super 50's, 60's &amp; 70's - Lynwood, CA
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is the space where Lynwood High Alumni from the 50’s to the 70’s can visit to see "what's up" with our classmates, friends, family, and others that remember growing up in Lynwood during the “wonder years.” What's so special about Lynwood you ask? Lynwood, CA, is a very special community located half-way between downtown LA and downtown Long Beach. This proximity to the big city of LA, and the So Cal beaches, made it a great place to grow up. For those of us that grew up there in the 50’s, 60’s and 70’s, we have many fond memories of life in Lynwood. Of course many of us went to the Lynwood schools, be it Lindbergh, Wilson, Abbott, Lincoln, Lugo, Mark Twain, Roosevelt, Washington, Will Rogers, Hosler Jr. High, and of course, Lynwood High. Or maybe one of the parochial schools, St. Paul’s Lutheran or St. Emydius Catholic School or Pius High School (Downey.) This Facebook space is the place for those memories. It is a place to network, look for old friends, and keep the spirit of Lynwood alive. Lets hear your stories about growing up in Lynwood. I know I have a few that I look forward to sharing. Got old photos or videos? Post them here, we’d love to see them. I just took a “memory” tour through Lynwood and took photos of my old school, my old home, my old church, and all that good stuff. You know what? Lynwood still looks pretty good. Different, yes, but I saw a lot of the pride in ownership that my Mom had when she bought our home on Louise St. in 1947. Can’t wait to see what everyone does with this space. Have fun, remember the good times, and cherish the great memories we all have. Who can join this group? Anyone that has fond memories of Lynwood. This should be a positive space to keep some great memories alive. Enjoy! As the description suggests, this group encourages positive interaction amongst members. Any comments deemed inappropriate or inflammatory will be removed and any member that abuses this forum will be blocked. Please, no religious or political posts. All of us love the community of Lynwood and we like to see it remembered in a positive light. Jerry Simmons, LHS Class of '74 Proudly born and raised in Lynwood, CA 
                </div>

                 This group is for homeschooling families of color that are looking for more opportunities to support and communicate with other homeschooling families.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for teachers who want to receive new, much needed classroom supplies and pay next to nothing. We also encourage you to share your experiences with NAEIR and provide other creative options to save money on classroom supplies. If you are not a member of NAEIR's Teacher Program, to join, all you have to do is complete the FREE Registration (you will set up your login ID and password at the time you submit your registration). After your registration is processed (and sometimes it takes a while) you will receive an email that your login ID and password are activated you will have access to millions of dollars’ worth of classroom supplies. The products are available for nominal handling charges and a small processing fee. Shipping is free. The only requirement is that your handling charges per request total $25 or greater. To learn more about the Teacher’s Program visit the NAEIR website at www.naeir.org. If you want to browse the items currently available, click on the “Shop NAEIR” button in the upper right hand corner of the Home Page. Members of the Teacher’s Program have access to all sections of the NAEIR shopping site, with the exceptions of Express and Big Book. The Teacher’s Program Registration form can be found on the Home Page. The sooner you get signed-up the sooner you can start getting classroom supplies . . . for next to nothing.

                 There is a better way to teach! Gameschooling is the practice of introducing and using games in education. Please read rules before joining. HOUSE RULES: .00 - Your admins are Meg, Penny, Michelle, &amp; Jonathan Key. Please feel free to contact us at any time via PM. (updated 8/24/2020) .05 - THERE WILL BE ADVERTISING but this is a privilege reserved only for admin. No advertising = no website = no group. I know it stinks, no one likes to be inundated with ads so we try to be sensitive to that and keep all deal posts in one thread so you can turn off notifications. 1. ALL ARE WELCOME BUT RECOMMENDATIONS MUST BE SECULAR. Non-secular posts will be removed. 2. BE EXCELLENT TO EACH OTHER. No name-calling, no rude or ignorant comments, no parenting of others, no criticizing other parenting or homeschooling styles. Admin can handle criticism, but we do ask that it be kept polite. We will remove &amp; ban members for aggressiveness. 2.5 BEHAVIORS WE WILL NOT ALLOW LIST: This list is not optional and a violation will lead to your removal. •Racism •Hate speech •Discrimination •Genderism •Sexism •Misogyny •Xenophobia •Willful ignorance •Jokes &amp; disparaging remarks about mental illness •Ableism •Ageism •Cruel words &amp; ideas •America-first language/resources (updated 8/24/2020) 3. NO ADVERTISING OF ANY KIND, except admin. This applies to: Kickstarter promotions, affiliate links that earn you money or rewards, sharing your/your child's YouTube channel, etc. Zero tolerance for Simply Fun &amp; Usborne reps advertising, sharing parties, sharing their store, asking people to contact them for sales. Questions? Let us know :) (updated 8/24/2020 for clarity) 4. Y’all, we love you. We’re fierce advocates for equal representation in gaming &amp; we’re also fierce advocates for mental health. YOUR LIFE IS VALUABLE! We’re always available if you need someone to chat with, provide a distraction, etc. We will gladly play you in some online/app games too! https://suicidepreventionlifeline.org/chat/ Optional: If you share a meme, please type the text of the meme as well.               <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Special Ed Mom Survival Guide: IEP, 504 and Parenting Support Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Please note, people who do not answer the questions will not be approved for membership. This is a place to talk about how to help your child be successful in life and in school. This group is managed by a former special education advocate who is also a mom and has found ways to get her children the right support. Questions about IEPs, 504s, schools refusing services are par for the course in this group. Members do not offer legal advice but can point you in the right direction to get support. This is not a political group. Those who share political posts or start political discussions will be removed without warning. Members share about our struggles with being a special needs parent, and we celebrate the wonderful moments when everything goes great. We support you in finding the best school support for your child, but we also encourage you to look for solutions outside of school to help your child cope or improve. In this group we support the idea of biomedical healing, therapies, medication and ways to help improve cognitive function and quality of life for our children. You are welcome to join if you disagree with these things, but do not criticize those asking for help in these areas. This group is for USA parents with children in special education. Because of privacy issues of parents, we do not admit members who are not parents of special needs children. We welcome parents of special needs children who are also professionals who support special needs kids. However, professionals who promote their business without permission will be removed without notice. I do not admit members who are pages or who have company names as their profile name. 
                </div>
               </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Reggio Inspired Early Childhood Educators
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome Amazing Early Childhood Educators! This is meant to be a place of support. It is a place to help you grow in your teaching journey and provide support along the way. Speaking of which, I have tons of free ebooks for you at http://fairydustteaching.com/library. SO HERE IS HOW THIS GROUP WORKS: 1. A NO-JUDGEMENT ZONE: This is a space full of incredible educators who are at different stages of their teaching journey. We like to keep it supportive so if you don't have something nice to say, please don't post it. Kindness matters. We have a zero tolerance policy for name calling, shaming or telling someone what they are doing is not okay or incorrect. 2. Promotional posts are not allowed unless arranged with the administrator of this group (Sally). **If we see something that looks like a promotion we reserve the right to delete it. ** 5. Please DO post about your teaching practice questions, ask for feedback, let us support you. 5. Please DO post about your challenges in both teaching and family so that we can show you that you are not alone, give you ideas and encouragement. 6. Please DO connect and collaborate, share your ideas, engage with the other awesome early childhood educators. We are a place of support and celebration. 7. Derogative posts or comments about race, religion, culture, sexual orientation, gender or identity will not be tolerated. This includes negative comments about parents, students, teachers, administrators, colleagues, or anyone in our group. 8. No Fairy Dust Teaching customer service questions posted here. Honestly - we probably won't see it. Any technical/account/service related questions should be emailed to: asksally@fairydustteaching.com, and not posted in the group. **By joining this group, you agree to be respectful of others in all posts and comments.** IMPORTANT POSTING NO-NOs (these will be deleted!): *Do not share video or photos that you did not take yourself or that you do not have permission to share. *No controversial or political posts. *No Sharing conversations outside of this group via screenshot. *Crowd source funding is not allowed. This includes Donor's Choose, Go Fund Me, *No prayer requests. *No Google Doc links. *No file sharing. *No FB live or FB Stories. So excited to have you here! Sally Haughey Founder of Fairy Dust Teaching
                </div>

                 The Preschool Toolbox
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is designed for teachers, caregivers, parents, and all who have an interest in teaching and caring for preschoolers. Please note: ALL comments are moderated to reduce the amount of SPAM to this community. Please be respectful of all members when commenting and sharing ideas. We value debate and lively discussion, but respectful discussion is mandatory regardless of personal opinions. Comments that are not respectful and professional, will be deleted. MEMBERS - *Website Owners and Bloggers may share self-promotional links ONLY when valid to sharing resources as a direct response to another's discussion question. ALL LINKS/PHOTOS/MEMES, etc. that are not relative to the discussion thread, will be deleted by admin. *Only photos of your own children may be shared. School photos of children MUST have the frontal views/faces of children blocked or disguised before approval. Questions concerning use of a FB Media release for sharing purposes should be directed to the admin. *We abide by COPYRIGHT regulations. If photos of activities are shared, they MUST be your own photos or contain links to the owner/creator/original website. If appropriate credit is not given, photos will be deleted by admin in accordance with COPYRIGHT rules. Come join us for lively discussion, preschool resources, and FUN!

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to our homeschool "pre-school" group. This is an informal group for mommas who want to follow a very loose, flexible curriculum for their toddlers and kindergarten age kiddos. **Note: you do not have to homeschool to be a part of this group! Anyone is welcome to get and share ideas. Last year we focused on a letter a week for 26 weeks. I will be loosely doing this again. I will post craft ideas, field trip ideas, and other fun activities to do with each letter (and then some!) Please feel free to share your ideas as well! Let's have some fun with this, ladies!

                 Loose Parts Play
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Loose Parts Play is all about sharing ideas and resources to use loose parts play in their homes and educational settings. Feel free to share pictures, videos, an other resources that may be helpful. Celebrate your success, ask questions for resources, and find solutions to issues you may find. Started by Dr. Carla Gull from www.insideoutsidemichiana.com as part of a project on Loose Parts Play at a local nature center. She works full time teaching beginning college classes at the University of Phoenix.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 K1/K2 Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 K1/K2 Group was created on April 14, 2013 to support those going through the K1/K2 route. Feel free to join! (SWA / SUPREME WEALTH ALLIANCE AND OTHER NETWORKING POSTS ARE NOT WELCOME HERE! THIS IS A VISA GROUP!!!) Main Objectives: 1. To share ideas and tips for processing of K1 / K2 petition and processes thereafter. 2. To share experiences of each visa journeys, life in Pinas and our slice of the American Pie. 3. To guide others who are processing their Petitions, Medical, Interview, SSN, Adjustment of Status, Application for Employment Document etc. 4. To share POE and travel tips. 5. To share anything under the sun that would be BENEFICIAL for everyone especially re: visa. :) Guidelines for posts and comments: 1. We have different dialects and origins (Kapampangan, Visaya, Batangeña, etc.) Please post or comment in Tagalog or English as much as possible so that everyone will understand and can join the conversation. 2. Posts photos, videos, statements highlighting K1/K2. 3. Sharing of own interests and activities are allowed; but to a minimal extent. No flooding or SPAMMING please. (SWA / SUPREME WEALTH ALLIANCE AND OTHER NETWORKING POSTS ARE NOT WELCOME HERE! THIS IS A VISA GROUP!!!) 4. There should be no discriminatory or derogatory posts and comments against any PERSON or group of persons, race, gender and religion. 5. Lewd, vulgar, obscene, profane or disrespectful posts and comments are not permitted. 6. The Administrators of the group reserve the right to block or remove any user and to hide or delete any posts or comments that do not comply with the above guidelines. To report, contact the following admins: April Grace Sabuerro Nash (Gingoog City, Mindanao | Homosassa, Florida) https://www.facebook.com/aprilgrace.s.demetillo Jhoe Calva Desnous (San Francisco, Surigao del Norte | Albuquerque, New Mexico) https://www.facebook.com/gillesjhoe Jinky Cubillan Anderson (Cavite | Fortwalton Beach Florida ) https://www.facebook.com/jinky.anderson22 Joanne Tresvalles Crispell (aka Misis Crispell) (Quezon City, Metro Manila | Vestal, New York) https://www.facebook.com/profile.php?id=526632265 Jocelyn Daria Curran (Pasay, Metro Manila | Midland, Texas / Middleburg, Florida) https://www.facebook.com/jhoi.daria Marie Aderlean (aka Kitty Kirsty) (Deerfield Beach, Florida) https://www.facebook.com/samanthaprinces Marsha Brunswick (Manila | Philadelphia, Pennsylvania) https://www.facebook.com/marshae918 Mylene Versoza Baker (Caramona, Camarines Sur | San Antonio, Texas) https://www.facebook.com/versoza2 Plyn Cash (Calatagan, Batangas | Harvest, Alabama) https://www.facebook.com/glenn.cash.9?fref=ts Richelle Sangcap Hernandez (Concepcion, Tarlac | Miami, Florida / Albuquerque, New Mexico) https://www.facebook.com/Richellesangcap Last edited: March 05, 2015 6:30AM EST

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Special Education Teacher Leaders
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 MISSION: To develop and empower special education teacher leaders. Leadership at the teacher level is as important as school leadership. You're never too young to be a great leader and you're never too old to be a better one. This group’s focus will be on building special education teacher leadership skills to effectively manage and supervise the other adults in their room, work with administrators, and collaborate with general education teachers and parents. ABOUT THE ADMIN: The group’s admin, Dr. Natasha Veale, is a professor of special education and special education program coordinator at a small, private college. She has been a special education teacher educator for 12 years. She was a special education teacher and teacher leader for just under 9 years. Dr. Veale’s doctorate is in Special Education Leadership and she is a certified John Maxwell Speaker, Coach, and Trainer. John C. Maxwell is a world-renowned leadership expert with over 90 books, primarily about leadership. Dr. Veale’s passion is to help prepare special education teachers to become the leaders they desire to be and empower the current leaders to become more effective. As an extension of the group, Dr. Veale will offer optional paid online courses, mastermind groups, and leadership trainings on various topics related to teacher leadership using John Maxwell’s leadership books and resources to help you grow as special education teacher leaders. GROUP GUIDELINES: Please feel free to email sensitive issues to drveale77@gmail.com. This group is a safe and supportive place, but confidential and personal matters should not be shared publicly. The post can be posted anonymously if necessary. -Inclusion: Anyone who wants to support the group mission, is willing to grow, and invest in themselves is welcome to join. Invite your SpEd friends! -Privacy: What's shared here stays here! -Respect: We realize there will be many viewpoints. Please write constructive posts that are not judgmental of others. Our goal is to build each other up as special education teacher leaders. Never be afraid to ask a question. -Conflict: Dr. Veale will politely ask that all interpersonal conflict initiated within the group be resolved privately between the parties involved, not publicly as to unnecessarily involve others. The main group rule is to please remain on the topic of leadership as it pertains to special education. This is a space to share about overall growth as a special education teacher leader in the school and field when working with the other adults, not about pedagogy. *** No spam or solicitations are allowed in this group. Solicitations are defined as posts that clearly do not align with the group mission or provide any tangible benefits to the group members. You will be warned once and removed upon a second violation. *** 
                </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Preschool &amp; Pre-K Teaching Ideas
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to our community! Preschool and Pre-K Teaching Ideas is a safe community where you can ask questions, offer support, and get actionable ideas for improving your teaching. Of course, we have a few rules to keep this space as focused and helpful as possible. Make sure you check them out to learn just how to get the most from our community! New? Let me introduce myself! I’m Anna Geiger, a former teacher (M.Ed.) now raising my six kids and supporting educators through my website, The Measured Mom. My site offers thousands of free resources for teaching preschool through third grade. You can check it out here: https://www.themeasuredmom.com/ Like what you see? Consider joining my membership site, where I release new printables, quick video trainings, and no-print resources every month. Learn more about The Measured Mom Plus here: https://membership.themeasuredmom.com/ This space is the place for you to get support, ask questions, and ultimately be the best teacher you can be while still having time to enjoy the rest of your life. HERE'S HOW THIS GROUP WORKS: Please DO NOT post self-promotions or spam. Links to your own website, business, and other Facebook groups are not allowed. Please DO be kind and courteous. We have a zero-tolerance policy for name calling, shaming, or bullying. Please DO NOT post links to files. If you'd like to share a link to a free online resource, post the link (not file) so others can download it for themselves. Do note that group admins may post files courtesy of The Measured Mom. Please DO NOT send private messages to admins or members of this group. Please DO NOT post or seek requests for Donors Choose, Go Fund Me, etc. Please STICK TO TEACHING. We look forward to getting to know you, but we ask that most posts pertain to teaching preschool and pre-K. Posts entirely off-topic (and anything about politics!) may be swiftly deleted. Please DO post about your teaching joys and challenges so your fellow educators can support you. Please DO connect and collaborate, share your ideas, and engage with other awesome educators. We are a place of support and celebration!
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Secular, Eclectic, Academic (SEA) Homeschoolers
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Secular Eclectic Academic Homeschoolers! We are a friendly, diverse community. Our motto is, "Our differences are our strength." We highly value the diversity each member brings to our group. The group is intended as a positive force, and only those people who want to have a constructive discussion should join. The group is open to people of any faith or lack thereof. We only discuss secular academics in this group. That does not mean people cannot discuss religion within education, but it has to be from the perspective of academics, and all resources discussed will be strictly secular. The definition used by Secular Eclectic Academic Homeschoolers for what constitutes secular academic materials can be found at seahomeschoolers.com/definitions-constitutes-secular-academic-materials/ Upon joining the group please read the group rules document found in the files. We have this group and several topic specific affiliated subgroups. This is the main group where we talk about all things academic. Once you are a member please feel free to join any of our subgroups that interest you. Links to these groups can be found at the top of the discussion page for this group, in the group files, and on our Public Facebook page. The current list of affiliated groups includes Secular Eclectic Academic Homeschoolers Chat Secular Eclectic Academic Homeschoolers Gifted and Twice-Exceptional Secular Eclectic Academic Homeschoolers Learning Challenges/Special Needs Secular Eclectic Academic Homeschoolers Preschool Secular, Eclectic, Academic MS/HS Homeschoolers (For parents) Secular Eclectic Academic Classical Secular Home Education Secular, Eclectic, Vegan Homeschoolers Secular Eclectic Academic Homeschoolers March For Science Secular Eclectic Academic LGBTQ Secular Eclectic Academic Homeschoolers Permaculture and Gardening Secular Eclectic Academic Homeschooling with Chronic Illness Secular Eclectic Academic Homeschoolers: Physics for Teens Secular Eclectic Academic Homeschoolers Teen Writing Group Secular Eclectic Academic Homeschoolers Tween Book Club Secular Eclectic Academic Homeschoolers Teen Book Club Secular Eclectic Academic Homeschoolers Adult Book Club Like our page, facebook.com/seahomeschoolers, you will find articles we think will be of interest to secular, eclectic homeschoolers, links to great resources, and exciting news. We have a website, www.seahomeschoolers.com, that is to have a place people can trust to find articles and products of benefit to the secular, eclectic, academic homeschool community. This link takes you to an article that explains how this group got started and why. seahomeschoolers.com/about/.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Teachers of the Blind and Visually Impaired
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group was created for Teachers of the visually impaired who share the passion of teaching students who are blind or visually impaired. Feel free to collaborate, ask questions, share stories related to the field, and learn from each other. We welcome teachers to share open position announcements, and tell about new technology or apps you are using, but it is asked that you refrain from advertising unless it is a workshop or conference announcement. Vendors and Staffing companies- if you are not a TVI, please do not request membership. Parents or individuals with a visual impairment that are not professionals in the field- WE LOVE YOU, but ask that you instead look for groups that are geared towards parents or eye conditions. There are many great active groups out there! This group receives membership requests daily, some of which are TVI's and some of which are not. If you are a TVI requesting permission to join, but have a private profile making it difficult for me to determine if you truly are a TVI, please send me a message.
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 #LearnEverywhere
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Schools are being canceled throughout the country, but that doesn’t mean learning needs to end. Education isn’t a place, learning happens everywhere! This is a community of resources, of support and access. Whether you’re a parent with a child at home, an educator in search of material, or a curious student, let’s seize this moment to share ideas, solutions and learning materials anyone can use at home. There’s no perfect solution and in this group, there’s no wrong answer – just humanity at its best. What are the cool ways your kids are spending their time? What are you doing as a teacher to keep your kids engaged? What projects are you as a parent doing with your kids? Let’s leverage this moment to create an everlasting community that believes we have the power to learn everywhere. By accessing or in any way using this Group owned by yes. every kid. (the “yes. every kid. Site” or “Web Site”), you agree to yes. every kid’s Privacy Policy and Terms of Use. If you do not agree to any aspect of the Privacy Policy or Terms of Use, please do not use the yes. every kid. Site. yes. every kid. may, in yes. every kid’s sole discretion, modify, or revise the Privacy Policy and Terms of Use at any time, and you agree to be bound by such modifications or revisions. Your continued use of the yes. every kid. Site / mobile application indicates your acceptance of the Privacy Policy, Terms of Use, and any changes therein. Privacy Policy: https://www.learneverywhere.org/privacy-policy/ Terms of Use: https://www.learneverywhere.org/terms/
                </div>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Common Sense Educators
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Common Sense Educators is a group of educators committed to creating a positive, collaborative culture of digital learning and digital citizenship in their classrooms, schools, or districts. Whether a classroom teacher, tech coach, librarian, homeschool teacher, preservice teacher, parent coordinator, or more -- you can connect with inspiring educators in this group! Website: https://www.commonsense.org/education/ Facebook: https://www.facebook.com/CommonSenseEducators/ Twitter: https://twitter.com/CommonSenseEd GROUP GUIDELINES: We welcome educators from all walks of life, whether you are a newbie or an expert in digital learning! Everyone is on their own journey and we can all share and learn from each other. Please use common sense (no pun intended!) and be a good digital citizen by respecting others, posting responsibly, and engaging responsibly and collaboratively. What we hope to accomplish: Foster professional growth and community by sharing your great posts. The best posts are the ones that: - Offer your feedback and point of view. - Explain pedagogy and practices. - Provide specific examples from your school, district or organization. - Offer an explanation of how you use digital tools to achieve learning goals. - Provide depth to the conversation and help move the discussion forward. - Make strong connections with mutual respect. We love lively conversations and healthy debate that helps us learn and grow. Just remember to always engage respectfully. - Give credit where credit is due. - Keep yourself and your fellow community members safe. We are an inclusive community that relies on your help. Please notify us if you see inappropriate content so we can address it immediately. What we won’t accept: - Anything obscene, hateful, defamatory, humiliating, or libelous. - Posts that target class, gender, age, sexual orientation, religion, national origin, weight or disability. - Posts that bash, make fun of, or vent about other educators, administrators, students, student work, parents, etc. - Illegal content or content that is not properly credited. - References and jokes about violence, sex, alcohol/drugs, etc. - Any sexual content, unless it’s related to sex education or issues such as how to handle cases of sexting in schools. - “Salesy” or repetitive promotion of your own books, tech tool, blog, social profile, etc. - Asks for financial contributions for projects/programs. - Ongoing comments that conflict with Common Sense Education’s mission. - Political bashing. Our admins reserve the right to delete posts/members who fail to follow our guidelines. Privacy: This is a private group. Group members can not share your posts on their personal pages. That said, please be mindful when sharing your work, especially if you are posting pictures of your students. We recommend not using students' names or showing faces unless you have permission from students' parents. Thank you!
                </div>
               </div>

                 AmblesideOnline
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 GROUP DESCRIPTION (required reading to join the FB group): Welcome to AmblesideOnline's Facebook page! Our primary purpose is to serve those who are actively using AO &amp; those interested in learning about AO. Therefore, we ask that you read these guidelines and answer ALL 3 of the questions presented to you within 24 hours (if you answer only 1, your membership will be denied): On topic: We are sure that you'll have lots to talk about and that there will be many questions. However, we aren't a general hsing group or a parenting group. Try to limit the topics of discussion to those directly related to CM or implementing AO. We are not here to help anybody *not* use AO. This is AO's group, &amp; we adhere to CM's methods. We will not debate the validity of CM methods here. Charlotte Mason's words are the final arbiter on CM methodology for such things as: what makes a book living, how to do language arts,how to schedule books etc. We also don't debate other homeschool methods &amp; curriculum here (there is room for that on the AO forum). If you have a complaint or criticism, please contact us privately: amblesideonlinemoderators@gmail.com -- All private correspondence will be discussed &amp; responded to privately. No buying and selling on our FB pages. Use the buying/selling area in the forum for that. No affiliate links. Anyone who appears to have joined with an agenda for promoting a website, product, or alternate homeschool method will be removed, as will those who ignore us &amp; attempt to use our group for profit, or repeatedly attempt to promote another method. In fact, though we operate with a light hand, Admins reserve the right to remove any posts for any reason, or to turn off commenting on a post. This includes but is not limited to: posts that have received plenty of helpful replies, are unrelated to AO, contentious, porn, or spam. CM was a Christian. So are we. Non-Christians are very welcome, but we don’t permit disrespectful treatment of our faith. Please remember FB's privacy cannot be guaranteed, search facilities are limited, organizing posts by topic is impossible. This group does not replace our forum or website. The website is AO's main online presence. You can homeschool using AO without joining the forum or fb, but you cannot homeschool using AO without reading our website. Links: AmblesideOnline: http://www.amblesideonline.org Forum: https://amblesideonline.org/forum/ Advisory Blog: http://archipelago7.blogspot.com/

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Thomas Jefferson High School, Los Angeles, CA Jefferson H.S. is located in South Central Los Angeles and has served this community since 1916. Over the last decades many accomplished individuals have attended our school, including choreographer Alvin Ailey, diplomat and Nobel Peace Prize winner Ralph Bunche, actress Dorothy Dandridge and jazz saxophonist Dexter Gordon. Many famous pop and jazz musicians attended Jefferson in the 1950s and 60s. Today, Jefferson strives to produce accomplished, skilled, and responsible graduates who will be ready to analyze and solve the problems of this increasingly diverse community in the 21st century.

                 Flexible Waldorf
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is designed for the parent or individual who is considered a "moderate" or "flexible" in the Waldorf philosophy. Our focus is Waldorf ONLY here. The flexible part will be outlined in our Flexible Waldorf Guidelines, so please read this FIRST before posting. There is a high tolerance level for religion (or spiritual preference) and all people of all ethnic backgrounds. We are here to share and learn. We also have a "Flexible Waldorf Archive" that is highly organized for everyone to benefit from using. Anthroposophical views are welcome here, as Waldorf education was founded on these principles. However, it is advised to consider that not all members will understand or agree with these. Each person can decide freely to accept or reject. ****However, we do not want debate on that topic here.**** In addition, we are here to reserve comments that would be considered discouraging. It is okay to debate and have an intelligent conversation about it. The main thing here is you exercise "The Golden Rule". You can share as much as you like here within the guidelines created. Remember, we are "flexible" here. Steiner promoted "freedom" and free will as a path to knowledge. We should always have the freedom to choose (exercise free will) what is best for our own lives and circumstances. “Our highest endeavor must be to develop free human beings who are able of themselves to impart purpose and direction to their lives. The need for imagination, a sense of truth, and a feeling of responsibility—these three forces are the very nerve of education.” ― Rudolf Steiner THIS GROUP DOES NOT ALLOW OTHER EDUCATION MODELS/METHODS TO BE DISCUSSED. THIS IS A WALDORF GROUP. Group Rules: https://www.facebook.com/notes/flexible-waldorf/group-rules/2521267728127924/

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Special Needs Homeschooling
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hello! This group is for those homeschooling their special needs child or seriously thinking about it. This group is an extension of my blog, www.specialneedshomeschooling.com and my book 'Homeschooling When Learning Isn't Easy' We have gifted, twice exceptional, autism, learning disabilities, cerebral palsy, genetic conditions, medical conditions you name it. We have all found one great thing homeschooling provides a wonderful, enriching environment for our child to learn. However there must be rules in a group this big to maintain a healthy group atmosphere. 1) this group is NOT a place to find people to sell your items/services 2) send messages/emails to other members degrading them or their personal decisions 3) misusing your status as a group member could get you ban from the group. 4) If you are a spammer, use profanity, deliberately hurtful, ect. I will warn you OR ban you at my discretion. Note for APPLYING: Anyone facing, considering, or learning at home is welcome. You MUST answer the questions or you will automatically be declined. Note for POSTING: Comments are moderated. If you post something take a moment to write WHY it's important to homeschooling or raising your special needs child. We are not medical or educational professionals this is an experience based parents group. If you are a professional please take any professional conversation off group. Thank you!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Pocket of Preschool Curriculum Facebook Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hello early childhood teacher friends! This group is a support group just for teachers who use Pocket of Preschool Curriculum. It's a place to collaborate, share, ask questions, learn, grow, and celebrate teaching using all things Pocket of Preschool! I'm the teacher author behind Pocket of Preschool. I will share links, products, and videos to help you teach your little learners (and have fun doing it too) using the Pocket of Preschool Curriculum. Please keep sharing threads related to Pocket of Preschool. Sorry friends but this is NOT a place for -Selling or Self Promotion (ex: TPT products, make up, cookware, leggings, ect.) -Job postings -Asking for other members' emails -Ask for donations (ex: GoFundMe, Donors Choose) -Message people privately to try and sell them anything. -Postcard exchanges -Discussions about other curriculum -All posts and answers must be in English. Admins may delete or remove members, photos, and/or threads at any time for not following group guidelines. Pocket of Preschool TPT Store: https://www.teacherspayteachers.com/Store/Pocket-Of-Preschool Blog/Website: http://www.pocketofpreschool.com/ Pocket of Preschool Facebook Page https://www.facebook.com/pocketofpreschool/ Newsletter Sign Up http://www.pocketofpreschool.com/p/newsletter.html

                 Website: http://www.vsauci.org Subscribe to our Newsletter: http://eepurl.com/dJa7hz VSA strives to preserve and promote the Vietnamese culture at UCI through creative and entertaining weekly meetings and by offering a wide range of social and cultural activities geared towards varying member talents and interests. The idea is to recognize that as most of us are Vietnamese/Americans, we are inherently connected to a culture with a vivid history of strength, art, pride, pain, and perseverance. VSA members can partake in various activities such as intramural sports, modern dance, traditional dance, a lion dance team, pool, singing, acting, and much more. Major events hosted annually include the Rose Pageant and VSA Culture Night, open to all students and surrounding communities.
